||- Graphic descriptions of any kind, including but not limited to eating disorders or self harm.
- Pornographic Content 
- Hate speech

- categorizing or profiling others' personalities||
- Anything that breaks discord's term of service or community guidelines, found here:
<https://discord.com/terms>, <https://discord.com/guidelines>


**The following topics are allowed, but must be censored/spoiler marked properly. These DO NOT belong in light channels for any reason:**


||- Sexual Assault
- Abuse
- Child abuse/pedophilia/incest
- Animal cruelty or animal death
- Self-harm and suicide
- Eating disorders, body hatred, and fat phobia
- Violence, including weapons
- Kidnapping and abduction
- Death or dying
- Drugs and alcohol abuse, including smoking
- Pregnancy/Childbirth
- Miscarriages/Abortion
- Blood
- COVID-19 and related conversation
- Mental illness discrimination and ableism
- Racism and racial slurs
- Sexism and misogyny
- Hateful language directed at religious groups (e.g., Islamophobia, - antisemitism)
- Transphobia and trans misogyny
- Homophobia and heterosexism
- Corporal punishment||

The word meds does not need to be spoilered but as soon as you go into specifics about what the medication is or the name of it, it requires spoilers such as ||pain meds|| or ||benzodiazepines||.

To spoiler something, place \|\| on either side of the word or phrase you wish to censor. If you fail to spoiler mark something, you will be asked to do so and potentially warned. Failure to properly censor on multiple occasions will result in a ban.
